The regex pattern for matching and stripping out low-order non-printable ASCII characters (ASCII 0-31) from string data would 
[\\x00-\\x08\\x0B\\x0C\\x0E-\\x1F]
^[^\\x09\\x0A\\x0D\\x20-\\x7E]+$
The regular expression to match and strip out low-order non-printable ASCII characters (ASCII 0-31) from string data prior to adding to an XML document, while excluding ASCII 9, 10, and 13, can be generated as follo
[&]amp;#x([0-1]?[0-9]|2[0-9]|3[01]);
[\\x00-\\x1A\\x1C-\\x1F]
[\\x00-\\x08\\x0B\\x0C\\x0E-\\x1F]
